if that guy's going down to zero , i'll know .	如果那傢伙要降到零 , 我會知道 。
and with computation and algorithms and predictive models , we will be able to see the future .	有了計算、演算法和預測模型 , 我們就能看到未來 。
you may think that's impossible .	你可能認為不可能 。
how can you predict the future ? that's really hard .	你要如何預測未來 ? 真的很困難 。
actually , no . with cars , it's not impossible .	事實上 , 不 , 車子 , 不是不可能的 。
cars are threedimensional objects that have a fixed position and velocity .	汽車是三維的物體 , 擁有固定的位置和速度 。
they travel down roads .	他們走在路上 。
often they travel on prepublished routes .	通常他們會走上預先發表的路線 。
it's really not that hard to make reasonable predictions about where a car's going to be in the near future .	其實 , 要做合理的預測 , 其實並不難預測在不久的將來 , 汽車會在哪裡發生 。
even if , when you're in your car and some motorcyclist comes bshoom ! 85 miles an hour down , lanesplitting i know you've had this experience that guy didn't " just come out of nowhere . "	即使 , 當你在車子裡 , 有些摩托車騎士過來了 , 每小時85英里 , 車道裝置 , 我知道你有過這樣的經驗 , 那個傢伙沒有 「 出去 」 。
that guy's been on the road probably for the last half hour .	那傢伙在路上 , 可能已經半小時了 。
right ? i mean , somebody's seen him .	對吧 ? 我的意思是 , 有人看過他 。
ten , 20 , 30 miles back , someone's seen that guy , and as soon as one car sees that guy and puts him on the map , he's on the map position , velocity , good estimate he'll continue going 85 miles an hour .	10、20、30英里後 , 有人看過那個傢伙 , 只要一輛車看到那個傢伙 , 把他放在地圖上 , 速度 , 估計他會以時速85英里的速度繼續下去 。
you'll know , because your car will know , because that other car will have whispered something in his ear , like , " by the way , five minutes , motorcyclist , watch out . "	你們會知道 , 因為你的車會知道 , 因為另一輛車會在他的耳朵上說: 「 順便一提 , 五分鐘 , 摩托車 , 看出來 。 」
you can make reasonable predictions about how cars behave .	你可以合理地預測汽車的行為 。
i mean , they're newtonian objects .	我的意思是 , 它們是牛頓的物品 。
that's very nice about them .	這對他們來說很棒 。
so how do we get there ?	所以 , 我們要如何做到 ?
we can start with something as simple as sharing our position data between cars , just sharing gps .	我們可以從簡單的開始 , 如分享車子間的位置資料 , 分享gps 。
if i have a gps and a camera in my car , i have a pretty precise idea of where i am and how fast i'm going .	如果我在車上有gps和攝影機 , 我有個很精確的概念 , 能知道我在哪裡 , 要走多快 。
with computer vision , i can estimate where the cars around me are , sort of , and where they're going .	有了電腦視覺 , 我可以估計我周圍的汽車在哪裡 , 哪裡 , 還有它們在哪裡 。
and same with the other cars .	其他車子也一樣 。
they can have a precise idea of where they are , and sort of a vague idea of where the other cars are .	他們可以精確地知道他們在哪裡 , 有點模糊的概念 , 知道其他車子在哪裡 。
what happens if two cars share that data , if they talk to each other ?	如果兩輛車共享這些資料 , 如果他們彼此交談 , 會如何 ?
i can tell you exactly what happens .	我可以告訴你們發生了什麼事 。
professor bob wang and his team have done computer simulations of what happens when fuzzy estimates combine , even in light traffic , when cars just share gps data , and we've moved this research out of the computer simulation and into robot test beds that have the actual sensors that are in cars now on these robots: stereo cameras , gps , and the twodimensional laser range finders that are common in backup systems .	鮑勃•威奇教授和他的團隊做了電腦模擬 , 來模擬當模擬混合時 , 甚至在輕型車輛上 , 只要分享gps資料 , 我們就把這個研究從電腦模擬中搬出來 , 進入機器人測試 , 讓這些機器人有真正的感測器 , 裝在這些機器人身上 , 像是車子:攝影機、gps , 和二維雷射測器 。
we also attach a discrete shortrange communication radio , and the robots talk to each other .	我們也連接了一台簡短的通訊無線電機 , 機器人彼此交談 。
when these robots come at each other , they track each other's position precisely , and they can avoid each other .	當這些機器人互相接觸時 , 它們會精確地追蹤彼此的位置 , 它們能避免彼此 。
we're now adding more and more robots into the mix , and we encountered some problems .	我們現在在混合中加入越來越多的機器人 , 我們遇到了一些問題 。
one of the problems , when you get too much chatter , it's hard to process all the packets , so you have to prioritize , and that's where the predictive model helps you .	其中一個問題是 , 當你收到太多章節時 , 很難處理所有的包裝 , 所以你得要先考慮 , 那就是預測模型協助你的地方 。
if your robot cars are all tracking the predicted trajectories , you don't pay as much attention to those packets .	如果你的機械汽車都在追蹤預測軌跡 , 你就不會注意到那些包裝 。
you prioritize the one guy who seems to be going a little off course .	你把那個看起來有點不好的傢伙做優先順序 。
that guy could be a problem .	那傢伙可能是個問題 。
and you can predict the new trajectory .	你可以預測新的軌跡 。
so you don't only know that he's going off course , you know how .	所以你不只知道他會走下路 , 你知道的 。
and you know which drivers you need to alert to get out of the way .	你知道你需要警告哪些司機才能離開 。
and we wanted to do how can we best alert everyone ?	我們想要怎麼做才能讓每個人更警告 ?
how can these cars whisper , " you need to get out of the way ? "	這些車怎麼會說: 「 你需要走出路 ? 」
well , it depends on two things: one , the ability of the car , and second the ability of the driver .	嗯 , 它取決於兩件事:一 , 汽車的能力 , 第二個駕駛的能力 。
if one guy has a really great car , but they're on their phone or , you know , doing something , they're not probably in the best position to react in an emergency .	如果一個人擁有一台很棒的車 , 但他們在手機上 , 或者 , 你知道 , 做點什麼 , 他們可能就不在緊急情況中反應最好的位置 。
so we started a separate line of research doing driver state modeling .	所以 , 我們開始了分離的研究 , 做司機國家模型 。
and now , using a series of three cameras , we can detect if a driver is looking forward , looking away , looking down , on the phone , or having a cup of coffee .	現在 , 用了一系列的三台攝影機 , 我們可以偵測出一系列的駕駛正向前 , 向下看 , 向下看 , 或喝一杯咖啡 。
we can predict the accident and we can predict who , which cars , are in the best position to move out of the way to calculate the safest route for everyone .	我們可以預測意外 , 我們可以預測誰 , 哪一輛車 , 最好的位置 , 不用去計算所有人最安全的路線 。
fundamentally , these technologies exist today .	基本上 , 這些技術今天就存在了 。
i think the biggest problem that we face is our own willingness to share our data .	我認為我們面臨的最大問題是我們自己願意分享我們的資料 。
i think it's a very disconcerting notion , this idea that our cars will be watching us , talking about us to other cars , that we'll be going down the road in a sea of gossip .	我想這是個非常令人不安的概念 , 這個想法:我們的車子會看著我們 , 跟我們談及其他車輛 , 我們會在一片八卦的海域下走下路 。
but i believe it can be done in a way that protects our privacy , just like right now , when i look at your car from the outside , i don't really know about you .	但我相信它可以用一種方式來保護我們的隱私 , 就像現在 , 當我從外面看你的車時 , 我不太了解你 。
if i look at your license plate number , i don't really know who you are .	如果我看你的牌牌數 , 我真的不知道你是誰 。
i believe our cars can talk about us behind our backs .	我相信我們的汽車可以在我們的背後談論我們 。
and i think it's going to be a great thing .	我想這會是件很棒的事 。
i want you to consider for a moment if you really don't want the distracted teenager behind you to know that you're braking , that you're coming to a dead stop .	我希望你花一點時間想想 , 如果你不想在你身後的青少年 , 知道你在煞車 , 那你就要走到停車場了 。
by sharing our data willingly , we can do what's best for everyone .	透過願意分享我們的資料 , 我們可以為每個人做最好的事 。
so let your car gossip about you .	所以 , 讓你的車往你的方向前走 。
it's going to make the roads a lot safer .	它會讓道路更安全 。
x prize founder peter diamandis talks about how he helped stephen hawking fulfill his dream of going to space by flying together into the upper atmosphere and experiencing weightlessness at zero g .	xprize創辦人彼得•戴曼迪迪迪迪諾所談到他如何幫助史蒂芬•霍金完成太空的夢想 , 透過一起飛進大氣層 , 體驗不到的體重 。
business , flight , science , short talk , space , technology , universe	商業 , 飛行 , 科學 , 短暫的演講 , 太空 , 宇宙 , 宇宙 。
peter diamandis on stephen hawking in zero g	彼得.狄桑迪斯在0g之中 , 採用史蒂芬.霍金 。
those of you who know me know how passionate i am about opening the space frontier .	認識我的人知道我對打開太空前線的熱情有多大 。
so when i had the chance to give the world's expert in gravity the experience of zero gravity , it was incredible .	所以當我有機會給世界地心引力的專家 , 這種無重力的體驗 , 實在是令人難以置信 。
and i want to tell you that story .	我想告訴各位這個故事 。
i first met him through the archon x prize for genomics .	我第一次見到他是基因組學的archonxprize 。
it's a competition we're holding , the second x prize , for the first team to sequence 100 human genomes in 10 days .	這是我們所舉辦的一個競賽 , 第二個xprize , 最早的團隊在10天內完成一百個人類基因組的序列 。
we have something called the genome 100 100 individuals we're sequencing as part of that .	我們有所謂的 「 基因組100個人 」 , 我們將它定序為其中的一部分 。
craig venter chairs that event .	克雷格•凡特的椅子 。
and i met professor hawking , and he said his dream was to travel into space .	我遇到了霍金教授 , 他說他的夢想是進入太空 。
and i said , " i can't take you there , but i can take you into weightlessness into zerog .	我說: 「 我不能帶你到那裡 , 但我可以帶你進入無重力的狀態 , 進入零 。
and he said , on the spot , " absolutely , yes . "	他說: 「 絕對 , 是的 。 」
well , the only way to experience zerog on earth is actually with parabolic flight , weightless flight .	唯一能體驗到地球上的0個要素 , 其實是帶著飛行 , 沒有重量的飛行 。
you take an airplane , you fly over the top , you're weightless for 25 seconds .	你搭飛機 , 飛過頂部 , 沒重25秒 。
come back down , you weigh twice as much .	回來 , 重量是兩倍 。
you do it again and again .	你再做一次 。
you can get eight , 10 minutes of weightlessness how nasa's trained their astronauts for so long .	你可以得到8、10分鐘無重量的無重力 , 美國太空總署長久以來訓練他們的太空人 。
we set out to do this .	我們開始做這件事 。
it took us 11 years to become operational .	我們花了11年才成為營運 。
and we announced that we were going to fly stephen hawking .	我們宣布要飛史蒂芬.霍金 。
we had one government agency and one company aircraft operator say , you're crazy , don't do that , you're going kill the guy .	我們有一家政府機關和一家公司飛機操作員說 , 你瘋了 , 不要這麼做 , 你要殺了那個傢伙 。
and he wanted to go .	他想要去 。
we worked hard to get all the permissions .	我們努力取得所有的許可 。
and six months later , we sat down at kennedy space center .	六個月後 , 我們在甘迺迪太空中心坐下來 。
we had a press conference , we announced our intent to do one zerog parabola , give him 25 seconds of zerog .	我們有一場記者會議 , 我們宣布我們的目的是要做一個0.25秒 , 給他25秒的0.
and if it went really well , we might do three parabolas .	如果一切順利的話 , 我們可能會做三個拋物玻璃 。
well , we asked him why he wanted to go up and do this .	嗯 , 我們問他為什麼他想上去做這件事 。
and what he said , for me , was very moving .	對我來說 , 他所說的非常動人 。
he said , " life on earth is at an everincreasing risk of being wiped out by disaster . . .	他說: 「 地球上的生命在不斷增加的危機上 , 被災難摧毀......
i think the human race doesn't have a future if it doesn't go into space .	我認為如果它不進入太空 , 人類就沒有未來 。
i therefore want to encourage public interest in space . "	所以我想鼓勵公眾對太空的興趣 。 」
we took him out to the kennedy space center , up inside the nasa vehicle , into the back of the zerog airplane .	我們把他帶到甘迺迪太空中心 , 在美國太空總署的車上 , 到零號飛機的後面 。
we had about 20 people who made donations we raised $150 , 000 in donations for children's charities who flew with us .	我們有大約二十個人捐款給十五萬美元給兒童慈善事業的捐款 。
a few tedsters here .	這裡有幾位tedtster 。
we set up a whole er .	我們設立了一整個伺服器 。
we had four emergency room doctors and two nurses on board the airplane .	我們有四個急診室的醫生和兩位護士登上飛機
we were monitoring his po2 of his blood , his heart rate , his blood pressure .	我們在監控他的血液、心跳、血壓 。
we had everything all set in case of an emergency ; god knows , you don't want to hurt this worldrenowned expert .	我們所有的事都發生在緊急情況下 , 上帝知道 , 你不想傷害這個世界知名的專家 。
we took off from the shuttle landing facility , where the shuttle takes off and lands .	我們從shuttle的降落設施中脫落 , 在那裡 , 太空梭起落和降落 。
and my partner byron lichtenberg and i carefully suspended him into zerog .	而我的另一半是lichtenberg , 我小心地把他納入0g 。
once he was there , [we] let him go to experience what weightlessness was truly like .	一旦他在那兒 , 讓他去體驗無重量的真實性 。
and after that first parabola , you know , the doc said everything is great . he was smiling , and we said go .	在第一個拋物機後 , 你知道的 , 醫生說所有東西都很棒 。 他微笑 , 然後我們說了 。
so we did a second parabola .	所以我們做了第二個拋物機 。
we actually floated an apple in homage to sir isaac newton because professor hawking holds the same chair at cambridge that isaac newton did .	事實上 , 我們讓艾薩克•牛頓爵士裝上了一顆蘋果 , 因為霍金教授在劍橋舉起相同的椅子 , 艾薩克•牛頓 。
and we did a fourth , and a fifth and a sixth .	我們做了第四個 , 第五個 , 第六個 。
and a seventh and an eighth .	第七次和第八次 。
and this man does not look like a 65yearold wheelchairbound man .	這位男士看起來不像六十五歲的輪椅人物 。
he was so happy .	他非常開心 。
we are living on a precious jewel , and it's during our lifetime that we're moving off this planet .	我們活在珍貴的珠寶寶寶寶寶寶寶寶寶寶寶寶寶寶寶寶寶寶寶寶寶寶寶寶寶寶寶寶寶寶寶寶寶寶寶寶寶寶寶寶寶寶寶寶寶寶寶寶寶寶寶
please join us in this epic adventure .	請加入我們這個史詩般的冒險 。
medical animator david bolinsky presents 3 minutes of stunning animation that show the bustling life inside a cell .	醫療動畫者davidbolinsky展示了3分鐘的驚人動畫 , 展示了細胞內的忙碌生活 。
design , entertainment , film , health , medicine , science , technology , visualizations	設計、娛樂、電影、健康、醫學、技術、視覺化、視覺化、視覺化、視覺化、視覺化 。
david bolinsky animates a cell	davidbolinnsky將細胞動畫成一個細胞
i'm a medical illustrator , and i come from a slightly different point of view .	我是醫學插圖師 , 我來自稍微不同的觀點 。
i've been watching , since i grew up , the expressions of truth and beauty in the arts and truth and beauty in the sciences .	自從我長大以來 , 我一直在觀察 , 在科學中 , 真相和美麗的表達 。
and while these are both wonderful things in their own right they both have very wonderful things going for them truth and beauty as ideals that can be looked at by the sciences and by math are almost like the ideal conjoined twins that a scientist would want to date .	雖然這兩樣東西都很美好 , 但它們都有很美好的事物 , 可以用科學和數學來觀察它們 , 它們的美 , 幾乎就像是最理想的雙胞胎 , 科學家會想要約會 。
these are expressions of truth as awefull things , by meaning they are things you can worship .	這些表達出真相是令人敬佩的 , 意思是 , 它們是你能崇拜的事物 。
they are ideals that are powerful . they are irreducible .	它們是強大的理想 。 它們是不可思議的 。
they are unique . they are useful sometimes , often a long time after the fact .	它們是獨一無二的 , 有時很有用 , 在事實之後很久 。
and you can actually roll some of the pictures now , because i don't want to look at me on the screen .	你現在可以翻一些照片 , 因為我不想在螢幕上看著我 。
truth and beauty are things that are often opaque to people who are not in the sciences .	真相和美是常常對那些不在科學領域的人而不太友善的 。
they are things that describe beauty in a way that is often only accessible if you understand the language and the syntax of the person who studies the subject in which truth and beauty is expressed .	它們是用一種形容美的方式來形容美麗的事物 , 通常只能在你了解語言和人的語音之間 , 研究了這個主題 , 哪些真相和美麗被表達出來的人 。
if you look at the math , e=mc squared , if you look at the cosmological constant , where there's an anthropic ideal , where you see that life had to evolve from the numbers that describe the universe these are things that are really difficult to understand .	如果你看看數學 , e=mc平方 , 如果你觀察宇宙的常數 , 那裡有一個人類的理想 , 在那裡 , 你可以看到生命必須從描述宇宙的數字進化出來 , 這些是非常難理解的 。
and what i've tried to do since i had my training as a medical illustrator since i was taught animation by my father , who was a sculptor and my visual mentor i wanted to figure out a way to help people understand truth and beauty in the biological sciences by using animation , by using pictures , by telling stories so that the things that are not necessarily evident to people can be brought forth , and can be taught , and can be understood .	自從我身為醫學插圖師 , 自從我被教導的動畫 , 他是雕塑家 , 以及我的視覺導師 , 我想要找出方法 , 來幫助人們了解生物科學的真相和美 , 藉由動畫 , 用圖像 , 講述故事 , 讓人們不見得會被帶給人 , 可以被教導 , 也可以被理解 。
students today are often immersed in an environment where what they learn is subjects that have truth and beauty embedded in them , but the way they're taught is compartmentalized and it's drawn down to the point where the truth and beauty are not always evident .	現今 , 學生常常被沉浸在一個環境中 , 他們學到的是 , 真相和美的主題 , 嵌入在他們身上 , 但他們教導的方式 , 是比較的 , 且它被拉近到真相和美 , 不見得都是證據的 。
it's almost like that old recipe for chicken soup where you boil the chicken until the flavor is just gone .	這就像是雞湯的老食譜 , 讓雞沸騰 , 直到味道消失了 。
we don't want to do that to our students .	我們不想對學生這樣做 。
so we have an opportunity to really open up education .	所以我們有機會真正開放教育 。
and i had a telephone call from robert lue at harvard , in the molecular and cellular biology department , a couple of years ago . he asked me if my team and i would be interested and willing to really change how medical and scientific education is done at harvard .	我在哈佛大學的robertlue接到一通電話 , 在幾年前的分子和細胞生物系系裡 , 他問我 , 我和我的團隊是否有興趣 , 願意真正改變哈佛大學醫學和科學教育的做法 。
so we embarked on a project that would explore the cell that would explore the truth and beauty inherent in molecular and cellular biology so that students could understand a larger picture that they could hang all of these facts on .	所以我們開始進行一項計畫 , 探索細胞 , 來探索分子和細胞生物學的真相與美 , 讓學生能了解他們能連結所有這些事實的更大照片 。
they could have a mental image of the cell as a large , bustling , hugely complicated city that's occupied by micromachines .	他們可以將細胞的心理影像當作一個大型、繁忙、複雜的城市 , 由微機械佔據 。
and these micromachines really are at the heart of life .	這些微機械在生命的核心 。
these micromachines , which are the envy of nanotechnologists the world over , are selfdirected , powerful , precise , accurate devices that are made out of strings of amino acids .	這些微機械人 , 是奈米技術專家的嫉妒 , 都是自主的 , 強大的 , 精準的 , 精確的裝置 , 是由胺基酸所組成的 。
and these micromachines power how a cell moves .	而這些微機械的力量 , 細胞如何移動 。
they power how a cell replicates . they power our hearts .	它們能控制細胞如何複製 。 它們能驅動我們的心臟 。
they power our minds .	它們能驅動我們的心智 。
and so what we wanted to do was to figure out how we could make this story into an animation that would be the centerpiece of biovisions at harvard , which is a website that harvard has for its molecular and cellular biology students that will in addition to all the textual information , in addition to all the didactic stuff put everything together visually , so that these students would have an internalized view of what a cell really is in all of its truth and beauty , and be able to study with this view in mind , so that their imaginations would be sparked , so that their passions would be sparked and so that they would be able to go on and use these visions in their head to make new discoveries and to be able to find out , really , how life works .	所以 , 我們想要做的是找出我們如何把這個故事做成一個動畫 , 一個在哈佛大學的生理空間中心 , 一個哈佛大學的網站 , 用來研究它的分子和細胞生物學的網站 , 加上所有的文字資訊 , 再加上所有的做法 , 再加上所有的做法 , 讓這些學生對它的真相和美有內在的看法的看法 , 並且能夠研究這個觀點 , 透過它們的角度 , 讓它們的腦海中發現它們的影像 。
so we set out by looking at how these molecules are put together .	所以我們開始研究這些分子是如何組合在一起的 。
we worked with a theme , which is , you've got macrophages that are streaming down a capillary , and they're touching the surface of the capillary wall , and they're picking up information from cells that are on the capillary wall , and they are given this information that there's an inflammation somewhere outside , where they can't see and sense .	我們和一個主題合作 , 也就是說 , 有一個巨噬細胞 , 它們在微血管下流 , 碰到微血管壁的表面 , 它們會接觸到微血管壁的細胞 , 收集在微血管壁上的細胞的資訊 , 它們會被送到外面有發炎的資訊 , 在那裡 , 它們無法看見和感知 。
but they get the information that causes them to stop , causes them to internalize that they need to make all of the various parts that will cause them to change their shape , and try to get out of this capillary and find out what's going on .	但他們得到的資訊 , 會讓他們停止 , 讓他們內化 , 讓他們能製造出各種各樣的零件 , 讓他們改變他們的形狀 , 試著脫離這個微血管 , 找出發生了什麼事 。
so these molecular motors we had to work with the harvard scientists and databank models of the atomically accurate molecules and figure out how they moved , and figure out what they did .	所以這些分子馬達我們必須和哈佛科學家和資料庫合作 , 用原子正確的分子來計算它們的移動 , 找出它們是怎麼移動的 , 找出它們做了什麼 。
and figure out how to do this in a way that was truthful in that it imparted what was going on , but not so truthful that the compact crowding in a cell would prevent the vista from happening .	想出如何用真相的方式來做這件事 , 這種事在那過程中發生了什麼事 , 但事實並非如此 , 細胞內的密切擁擠會阻止病毒的發生 。
and so what i'm going to show you is a threeminute reader's digest version of the first aspect of this film that we produced . it's an ongoing project that's going to go another four or five years .	接下來我要給你們看的是一個三分鐘的讀者的消化版本 , 是我們製作的這部電影的第一個面向 。 這是一個持續進行的專案計畫 , 將會再四五年 。
and i want you to look at this and see the paths that the cell manufactures these little walking machines , they're called kinesins that take these huge loads that would challenge an ant in relative size .	我希望你們看看 , 看到細胞製造這些步行機器的路徑 , 稱為 「 松樹 」 , 採用這些巨大的載荷 , 以相對尺寸來挑戰螞蟻 。
run the movie , please .	請播放這部電影 。
but these machines that power the inside of the cells are really quite amazing , and they really are the basis of all life because all of these machines interact with each other .	但這些能驅動細胞內部的機器是很了不起的 , 它們其實是所有生命的基礎 , 因為這些機器互相交流 。
they pass information to each other .	他們互相傳遞資訊 。
they cause different things to happen inside the cell .	它們會造成不同的事情發生在細胞內 。
and the cell will actually manufacture the parts that it needs on the fly , from information that's brought from the nucleus by molecules that read the genes .	細胞會製造它需要在果蠅身上所需的部分 , 由細胞核裡的分子所產生的資訊來製造 , 以讀取基因的分子 。
no life , from the smallest life to everybody here , would be possible without these little micromachines .	沒有生命 , 從最小的生命 , 到這裡的每個人 , 都沒有這些微機械 。
in fact , it would really , in the absence of these machines , have made the attendance here , chris , really quite sparse .	事實上 , 在缺乏這些機器的情況下 , 克里斯的出席率真的很大 。
this is the fedex delivery guy of the cell .	這是細胞的fedex遞送者 。
this little guy is called the kinesin , and he pulls a sack that's full of brand new manufactured proteins to wherever it's needed in the cell whether it's to a membrane , whether it's to an organelle , whether it's to build something or repair something .	這個小傢伙稱之為 「 海底 」 , 他拉了一包裝滿全新的製造蛋白質到細胞所需的任何地方 , 不論是細胞膜 , 不論是組織 , 不論是建構或修復東西 。
and each of us has about 100 , 000 of these things running around , right now , inside each one of your 100 trillion cells .	我們每個人都有大約十萬個這種東西在四處跑來跑去 , 現在 , 在你一百兆個細胞裡面 。
so no matter how lazy you feel , you're not really intrinsically doing nothing .	所以 , 不論你有多懶惰 , 本質上你什麼都不做 。
so what i want you to do when you go home is think about this , and think about how powerful our cells are .	所以當你回家時 , 我希望你們想想這一點 , 想想我們的細胞有多強大 。
and think about some of the things that we're learning about cellular mechanics .	想想看我們所學到的細胞機制 。
once we figure out all that's going on and believe me , we know almost a percent of what's going on once we figure out what's going on , we're really going to be able to have a lot of control over what we do with our health , with what we do with future generations , and how long we're going to live .	一旦我們搞懂了一切 , 相信我 , 我們就知道 , 一旦我們搞清楚發生了什麼事 , 我們就能夠掌握許多控制權 , 掌握我們的健康 , 和我們未來的世代 , 以及我們將要活多久 。
and hopefully we'll be able to use this to discover more truth , and more beauty .	希望我們能用它來發現更多真相 , 和更多美 。
but it's really quite amazing that these cells , these micromachines , are aware enough of what the cell needs that they do their bidding .	但非常令人驚訝的是 , 這些細胞 , 這些微機械 , 都知道細胞所需的細胞所需的作用 。
they work together . they make the cell do what it needs to do .	他們一起工作 , 讓細胞做它所需的做法 。
and their working together helps our bodies huge entities that they will never see function properly .	他們一起工作 , 協助我們身體龐大的實體 , 他們永遠不會看到適當的功能 。
enjoy the rest of the show . thank you .	享受其餘的節目 。 謝謝 。
becky blanton planned to live in her van for a year and see the country , but when depression set in and her freelance job ended , her camping trip turned into homelessness . in this intimate talk , she describes her experience of becoming one of america's working homeless .	beckybranton計劃在她的車上住了一年 , 看到了這個國家 , 但當憂鬱的設定時 , 她的營地工作結束時 , 她的營地變成無家可歸的人 。 在這個親密的演講中 , 她描述了她成為美國無家可歸者的經驗 。
adventure , happiness , life , personal growth , poverty , social change , society , storytelling	冒險 , 快樂 , 人生 , 個人的成長 , 貧窮 , 社會改變 , 說故事 , 說故事 。
becky blanton: the year i was homeless	beckyblanton:那一年 , 我是無家可歸的那一年 , 我無家可歸 。
i'm a writer and a journalist , and i'm also an insanely curious person , so in 22 years as a journalist , i've learned how to do a lot of new things .	我是作家和記者 , 我也是個非常好奇的人 , 所以 , 身為記者 , 我學會了很多新事 。
and three years ago , one of the things i learned how to do was to become invisible .	三年前 , 我學到的其中一件事 , 就是變得看不見 。
i became one of the working homeless .	我成了工作無家可歸者之一 。
i quit my job as a newspaper editor after my father died in february of that same year , and decided to travel .	我辭掉我父親在同一年二月去世的報紙編輯工作 , 決定去旅行 。
his death hit me pretty hard .	他的死亡讓我非常難受 。
and there were a lot of things that i wanted to feel and deal with while i was doing that .	在我這麼做時 , 有很多我想要感受和處理的事物 。
i've camped my whole life . and i decided that living in a van for a year to do this would be like one long camping trip .	我一生都在營運 。 我決定住在車上 , 住了一年 , 去做這個 , 會是一趟很長的露營旅程 。
so i packed my cat , my rottweiler and my camping gear into a 1975 chevy van , and drove off into the sunset , having fully failed to realize three critical things .	所以 , 我把我的貓包起來 , 我的腐爛鐵絲網和我的露營裝備 , 送到1975年的雪梨旅行車上 , 開到陽光下 , 完全沒有意識到三件重要的事 。
one: that society equates living in a permanent structure , even a shack , with having value as a person .	第一:社會將生活在一個永久的結構中 , 甚至是一個收藏 , 一個人擁有價值 。
two: i failed to realize how quickly the negative perceptions of other people can impact our reality , if we let it .	第二:我沒有意識到 , 其他人的負面觀點能影響我們的現實 , 如果我們允許它的話 。
three: i failed to realize that homelessness is an attitude , not a lifestyle .	三:我沒意識到 , 無家可歸是態度 , 不是生活方式 。
at first , living in the van was great .	一開始 , 住在車上是很棒的 。
i showered in campgrounds . i ate out regularly .	我在營地洗澡 , 我常常吃東西 。
and i had time to relax and to grieve .	我有時間放鬆和悲慟 。
but then the anger and the depression about my father's death set in .	但接著 , 我父親死亡的憤怒和憂鬱 。
my freelance job ended . and i had to get a fulltime job to pay the bills .	我的自由工作終止了 。 我必須得到全職的工作來支付帳單 。
what had been a really mild spring turned into a miserably hot summer .	今年春天發生了一件非常溫和的夏天 。
and it became impossible to park anywhere without being very obvious that i had a cat and a dog with me , and it was really hot .	在任何地方 , 都無法公園 , 很明顯的 , 我有一隻貓 , 一隻狗 , 和我在一起 , 真的很熱 。
the cat came and went through an open window in the van .	貓來了 , 穿過車窗的窗戶 。
the doggy went into doggy day care .	狗狗進入狗狗的日子照護 。
whenever i could , i used employee showers in office buildings and truck stops .	每當我能做到時 , 我都會用在辦公大樓的員工和卡車站 。
or i washed up in public rest rooms .	或是我在公共場所洗澡 。
nighttime temperatures in the van rarely dropped below 80 degrees fahrenheit , making it difficult or impossible to sleep .	夜班的車溫度很少下降到華氏80度以下 , 讓它難以入眠 。
food rotted in the heat .	食物在熱氣中腐爛 。
ice in my ice chest melted within hours , and it was pretty miserable .	冰層的冰層在幾小時內就融化了 , 這相當悲慘 。
i couldn't afford to find an apartment , or couldn't afford an apartment that would allow me to have the rottweiler and the cat .	我負擔不起去找公寓 , 或買不起一間公寓 , 讓我能夠擁有腐爛的船隻和貓 。
and i refused to give them up , so i stayed in the van .	我拒絕放棄他們 , 所以我待在車上 。
and when the heat made me too sick to walk the 50 feet to the public restroom outside my van at night , i used a bucket and a trash bag as a toilet .	當暖氣使我太生病時 , 走在車外的五十英尺外的公共廁所 , 我用桶子和垃圾袋當廁所 。
when winter weather set in , the temperatures dropped below freezing . and they stayed there .	當冬天氣候發生時 , 溫度降到冰凍之下 , 他們留在那裡 。
and i faced a whole new set of challenges .	我面對了一系列新的挑戰 。
i parked a different place every night so i would avoid being noticed and hassled by the police .	每天晚上我停在不同的地方 , 這樣我會避免被警察注意到、被警察帶走 。
i didn't always succeed .	我並不總是成功的 。
but i felt out of control of my life .	但我無法控制我的人生 。
and i don't know when or how it happened , but the speed at which i went from being a talented writer and journalist to being a homeless woman , living in a van , took my breath away .	我不知道何時何時或如何發生 , 但是我從一個有才華的作家和記者轉變成一個無家可歸的女子 , 住在車上 , 帶著我的呼吸 。
i hadn't changed . my i . q . hadn't dropped .	我還沒改變 , 智商也沒掉下來 。
my talent , my integrity , my values , everything about me remained the same .	我的才華、我的完整性、我的價值觀 , 所有關於我的事都一樣 。
but i had changed somehow .	但我已經改變了 。
i spiraled deeper and deeper into a depression .	我將更深層、更深入到憂鬱中 。
and eventually someone referred me to a homeless health clinic .	最終有人把我稱為無家可歸的健康診所 。
and i went . i hadn't bathed in three days .	我去了 。 三天內 , 我沒有洗澡 。
i was as smelly and as depressed as anyone in line .	我和排隊中的任何人一樣感到沮喪和沮喪 。
i just wasn't drunk or high .	我只是不喝醉或喝醉 。
and when several of the homeless men realized that , including a former university professor , they said , " you aren't homeless . why are you really here ? "	當幾個無家可歸的人意識到 , 包括前一名大學教授 , 他們說: 「 你不是無家可歸 , 你為什麼在這裡 ? 」
other homeless people didn't see me as homeless , but i did .	其他無家者沒有把我視為無家可歸的人 , 但我做到了 。
then the professor listened to my story and he said , " you have a job . you have hope .	接著 , 教授會聽我的故事 , 他說: 「 你有工作 , 你有希望 。
the real homeless don't have hope . "	真正的無家可歸沒有希望 。 」
a reaction to the medication the clinic gave me for my depression left me suicidal . and i remember thinking , " if i killed myself , no one would notice . "	對於我憂鬱症所造成的藥物產生的反應 , 讓我自殺了 。 我記得在想: 「 如果我殺了我自己 , 沒有人會注意到 。 」
a friend told me , shortly after that , that she had heard that tim russert , a nationally renowned journalist , had been talking about me on national t . v .	不久之後 , 一位朋友告訴我 , 她聽說提姆•羅斯特 , 全國性的新聞記者 , 一直在談論我國家電視台 。
an essay i'd written about my father , the year before he died , was in tim's new book .	我寫了一篇關於我父親的文章 , 在他死前的那一年 , 在提姆的新書中 。
and he was doing the talk show circuit . and he was talking about my writing .	他正在做演說電路 。 他在談論我的寫作 。
and when i realized that tim russert , former moderator of " meet the press , " was talking about my writing , while i was living in a van in a walmart parking lot , i started laughing .	當我了解到 , timrusert之前的 「 見面新聞 」 的主持人 , 談到我的寫作 , 當我住在沃爾瑪停車場時 , 我開始大笑 。
i started laughing because it got to the point where , was i a writer , or was i a homeless woman ?	我開始笑 , 因為它已經到了我是作家 , 還是我是無家可歸的女性 ?
so i went in the bookstore . and i found tim's book .	所以我去了書店 , 找到提姆的書 。
and i stood there . and i reread my essay .	我站在那裡 , 重拾我的短文 。
because i was a writer .	因為我是個作家 。
i was a writer .	我是個作家 。
shortly after that i moved back to tennessee .	在那之後不久 , 我搬回田納西 。
i alternated between living in a van and couch surfing with friends .	我和朋友一起住在旅行車和沙發衝浪之間的區別 。
and i started writing again .	我又開始寫作了 。
by the summer of the following year i was a working journalist .	明年夏天 , 我是一名工作記者 。
i was winning awards . i was living in my own apartment .	我在獲獎 。 我住在我自己的公寓裡 。
i was no longer homeless .	我不再無家可歸 。
and i was no longer invisible .	我不再隱形了 。
thousands of people work full and parttime jobs , and live in their cars .	數以千計的人全職工作 , 同時也在他們的車裡生活 。
but society continues to stigmatize and criminalize living in your vehicle or on the streets .	但社會仍然將生活在交通工具或街上的犯罪化和犯罪化 。
so the homeless , the working homeless , primarily remain invisible .	所以無家可歸 , 工作無家可歸 , 主要是看不見的 。
but if you ever meet one , engage them , encourage them , and offer them hope .	但如果你曾經見過他們 , 讓他們參與 , 鼓勵他們 , 並提供他們希望 。
the human spirit can overcome anything if it has hope .	人類的精神可以克服任何事情 , 如果它有希望的話 。
and i'm not here to be the poster girl for the homeless .	我不是來這裡為無家可歸的無家可歸女性 。
i'm not here to encourage you to give money to the next panhandler you meet .	我不是來這裡鼓勵你們把錢給下一個乞討者 。
but i am here to tell you that , based on my experience , people are not where they live , where they sleep , or what their life situation is at any given time .	但我來這裡要告訴各位 , 根據我的經驗 , 人們不住在他們居住的地方 , 睡在哪裡 , 或他們生活的任何時候 。
three years ago i was living in a van in a walmart parking lot , and today i'm speaking at ted .	三年前 , 我住在walmart停車場 , 今天我在ted演講 。
hope always , always finds a way . thank you .	希望總是找到方法 。 謝謝 。
at tedxchange , thailand's " mr . condom , " mechai viravaidya , walks us through the country's bold plan to raise its standard of living , starting in the 1970s . first step: population control . and that means a lot of frank , funny and very effective talk about condoms .	在tedxchange , 泰國的 「 保險套先生 」 , 墨西哥維拉瓦達 , 走過全國大膽的計畫 , 提升生活水準 , 在1970年代開始 , 第一階段:人口控制 。 這意味著很多富蘭克 , 很有趣 , 非常有效地談論保險套 。
culture , global issues , health , population , science	文化、全球性議題、健康、人口、科學、科學、科學、文化、文化、健康、人口、人口、人口、
mechai viravaidya: how mr . condom made thailand a better place	墨西哥維拉瓦伊達:保險套先生如何讓泰國成為更好的地方 , 一個更好的地方 。
now , when i was a young man 40 years ago , the country was very , very poor with lots and lots and lots of people living in poverty .	四十年前 , 當我還是個年輕人時 , 這個國家非常非常貧窮 , 有許多人生活在貧窮之中 。
we decided to do something about it , but we didn't begin with a welfare program or a poverty reduction program .	我們決定要做點什麼 , 但我們不是從福利計畫開始 , 或減少貧窮計畫開始 。
but we began with a familyplanning program , following a very successful maternal child health activity , sets of activities .	但我們從一個家庭普遍計畫開始 , 以一個非常成功的孕育兒童健康活動 , 一組活動 。
so basically , no one would accept family planning if their children didn't survive .	基本上 , 沒有人會接受家庭規劃 , 如果他們的孩子沒有存活的話 。
so the first step: get to the children , get to the mothers , and then follow up with family planning .	所以 , 第一步 , 帶到孩子們 , 到母親那裡 , 然後跟著家人計畫 。
not just child mortality alone , you need also family planning .	不僅僅是兒童死亡率 , 你還需要家庭規劃 。
now let me take you back as to why we needed to do it .	現在 , 讓我帶各位回到我們為什麼需要這麼做 。
in my country , that was the case in 1974 .	在我的國家 , 那是1974年的案例 。
seven children per family tremendous growth at 3 . 3 percent .	家庭平均成長7個孩子 , 百分之3.3% 。
there was just no future .	沒有未來 。
we needed to reduce the population growth rate .	我們需要減少人口成長率 。
so we said , " let's do it . "	所以我們說: 「 咱們來做吧 。 」
the women said , " we agree . we'll use pills , but we need a doctor to prescribe the pills , " and we had very , very few doctors .	女性說: 「 我們同意 , 我們會使用藥丸 , 但我們需要醫生來開藥 。 」 我們的醫生非常少 。
we didn't take no as an answer ; we took no as a question .	我們沒有把答案當作一個答案 , 我們不把問題當作一個問題 。
we went to the nurses and the midwives , who were also women , and did a fantastic job at explaining how to use the pill .	我們去了護士和助產士 , 她們也是女性 , 做了一個很棒的工作 , 解釋如何使用藥丸 。
that was wonderful , but it covered only 20 percent of the country .	那真是太棒了 , 但它涵蓋了全國的20% 。
what do we do for the other 80 percent leave them alone and say , " well , they're not medical personnel . "	我們為其他80%的人做些什麼 , 讓他們獨自一人說: 「 嗯 , 他們不是醫療人員 。 」
no , we decided to do a bit more .	不 , 我們決定再做一點 。
so we went to the ordinary people that you saw .	所以我們去找一般人 。
actually , below that yellow sign i wish they hadn't wiped that , because there was " cocacola " there .	其實 , 在那黃色標誌下面我希望他們沒有報導 , 因為那裡有 「 可口可樂 」 。
we were so much bigger than cocacola in those days .	我們當時比可口可樂還要大很多 。
and no difference , the people they chose were the people we chose .	沒有差別 , 他們選的人是我們選的人 。
they were wellknown in the community , they knew that customers were always right , and they were terrific , and they practiced their family planning themselves .	他們在社區中很知名 , 他們知道客戶總是對的 , 他們很棒 , 他們練習自己的家庭規劃 。
so they could supply pills and condoms throughout the country , in every village of the country .	所以 , 他們可以在全國各地提供藥品和保險套 , 遍及全國各個村落 。
so there we are . we went to the people who were seen as the cause of the problem to be the solution .	所以 , 我們就在那裡 。 我們去找那些被視為是問題的原因 , 去解決問題的人 。
wherever there were people and you can see boats with the women , selling things here's the floating market selling bananas and crabs and also contraceptives wherever you find people , you'll find contraceptives in thailand .	不論在哪裡 , 都有人 , 你都能看到女人的船 , 販賣的是漂浮的市場賣香蕉和螃蟹 , 還有避孕用品 , 不論你在泰國哪裡 , 你都會找到人 , 你會在泰國找到避孕用品 。
and then we decided , why not get to religion because in the philippines , the catholic church was pretty strong , and thai people were buddhist .	接著 , 我們決定不要宗教 , 因為在菲律賓 , 天主教教會非常強壯 , 泰國人是佛教徒 。
we went to them and they said , " look , could you help us ? "	我們去找他們 , 他們說: 「 看 , 你能幫我們嗎 ? 」
i'm there the one in blue , not the yellow holding a bowl of holy water for the monk to sprinkle holy water on pills and condoms for the sanctity of the family .	我在那裏 , 藍色的那個 , 不是黃色的黃色 , 拿著一碗神聖的水 , 來把水灑在藥丸和保險套上 , 給家人的聖潔 。
and this picture was sent throughout the country .	這張照片被送到全國各地 。
so some of the monks in the villages were doing the same thing themselves .	所以 , 村子裡的一些僧侶也在做同樣的事 。
and the women were saying , " no wonder we have no sideeffects .	女性說: 「 難怪我們沒有副作用 。
it's been blessed . "	它被祝福了 。 」
that was their perception .	那是他們的感知 。
and then we went to teachers .	接著 , 我們去找老師 。
you need everybody to be involved in trying to provide whatever it is that make humanity a better place .	你需要每一個人 , 試著提供任何能讓人性變得更好的地方 。
so we went to the teachers .	所以我們去找老師 。
over a quarter of a million were taught about family planning with a new alphabet a , b for birth , c for condom , i for iud , v for vasectomy .	超過25萬人被教導要做家庭規劃 , 要有新字母a、出生、保險套、ud、虛擬切除術 。
and then we had a snakes and ladders game , where you throw dice .	然後我們有了一支蛇和梯子遊戲 , 讓你丟去的地方 。
if you land on anything profamily planning , you move ahead .	如果你降落在很棒的規劃上 , 你就會往前走 。
like , " mother takes the pill every night .	比如 「 媽媽每天晚上都會吃藥丸 。
very good , mother . move ahead .	非常好 , 媽媽 , 往前走 。
uncle buys a condom . very good , uncle . move ahead .	叔叔買保險套 , 非常好 , 叔叔 , 向前走 。
uncle gets drunk , doesn't use condom . come back , start again . "	叔叔喝醉 , 不用保險套 , 再來 , 再來 。 」
again , education , class entertainment .	再一次 , 教育 , 階級娛樂 。
and the kids were doing it in school too .	孩子們也在學校做這件事 。
we had relay races with condoms , we had children's condomblowing championship .	我們有保險套和保險套相關的競賽 , 我們有兒童保險套的冠軍 。
and before long , the condom was know as the girl's best friend .	很久以前 , 保險套就是女孩最好的朋友 。
in thailand , for poor people , diamonds don't make it so the condom is the girl's best friend .	在泰國 , 對窮人來說 , 鑽石不會把它變成這樣 , 所以保險套就是女孩最好的朋友 。
we introduced our first microcredit program in 1975 , and the women who organized it said , " we only want to lend to women who practice family planning .	我們在1975年介紹我們的第一個小額貸款計畫 , 那些組織它的女性說: 「 我們只想借錢給實踐家庭計畫的女性 。
if you're pregnant , take care of your pregnancy .	如果你懷孕了 , 照顧懷孕 。
if you're not pregnant , you can take a loan out from us . "	如果你沒有懷孕 , 你就可以把貸款從我們身上拿出來 。 」
and that was run by them .	他們就是這樣運作的 。
and after 35/36 years , it's still going on .	過了35/36年之後 , 仍然持續下去 。
it's a part of the village development bank ; it's not a real bank , but it's a fund microcredit .	它是村落發展銀行的一部分 ; 它不是真正的銀行 , 而是基金的小額貸款 。
and we didn't need a big organization to run it it was run by the villagers themselves .	我們不需要一個大型組織來經營它 , 由村民們自己經營 。
and you probably hardly see a thai man there , it's always women , women , women , women .	你可能看不到一個泰國男人 , 總是女人 , 女人 , 女人 。
and then we thought we'd help america , because america's been helping everyone , whether they want help or not .	接著 , 我們想我們會協助美國 , 因為美國的人民 , 不論他們想要協助 , 不論他們是否想要協助 。
and this is on the fourth of july .	這是七月四號 。
we decided to provide vasectomy to all men , but in particular , american men to the front of the queue , right up to the ambassador's residence during his [unclear] .	我們決定為所有男人提供放射性切除術 , 尤其是 , 美國男士們到皇室前 , 就在大使館的附近 。
and the hotel gave us the ballroom for it very appropriate room .	飯店給了我們那間非常適合的房間 。
and since it was near lunch time , they said , " all right , we'll give you some lunch .	既然是午餐時間 , 他們說: 「 好 , 我們會給你一些午餐 。
of course , it must be american cola .	當然 , 這一定是美國可樂 。
you get two brands , coke and pepsi .	你有兩個品牌 , 可口可樂和百事可樂 。
and then the food is either hamburger or hotdog . "	然後食物也不是漢堡或熱狗 。 」
and i thought a hotdog will be more symbolic .	我覺得熱狗比較象徵 。
and here is this , then , young man called willy bohm who worked for the usaid .	這裡是這位年輕人 , 威利•鮑姆 , 他為美國援助工作 。
obviously , he's had his vasectomy because his hotdog is half eaten , and he was very happy .	很顯然 , 他有放大的選擇 , 因為他的熱狗半吃了一半 , 他非常開心 。
it made a lot of news in america , and it angered some people also .	它在美國製作了很多新聞 , 同時也讓一些人感到憤怒 。
i said , " don't worry . come over and i'll do the whole lot of you . "	我說: 「 別擔心 , 請過來 , 我會做你們很多人 。 」
in all this thing , from seven children to 1 . 5 children , population growth rate of 3 . 3 to 0 . 5 .	在這一切中 , 從七個孩子到1.5個孩子 , 人口成長率是3.3到0.5 。
you could call it the cocacola approach if you like it was exactly the same thing .	你可以稱它為可口可樂的方法 , 如果你喜歡它是完全一樣的 。
i'm not sure whether cocacola followed us , or we followed cocacola , but we're good friends .	我不確定可口可樂是否跟著我們 , 或我們追蹤可口可樂 , 但我們是好朋友 。
and so that's the case of everyone joining in .	這就是每個人加入的案例 。
we didn't have a strong government . we didn't have lots of doctors .	我們沒有強大的政府 , 我們沒有很多醫生 。
but it's everybody's job who can change attitude and behavior .	但每個人都能改變態度和行為 。
then aids came along and hit thailand , and we had to stop doing a lot of good things to fight aids .	接著 , 愛滋病來到泰國 , 我們必須停止做很多好事來對抗愛滋病 。
but unfortunately , the government was in denial , denial , denial .	但不幸的是 , 政府在否認、否認、否認 。
so our work wasn't affected .	所以我們的作品沒有受到影響 。
so i thought , " well , if you can't go to the government , go to the military . "	所以我想: 「 嗯 , 如果你不能去政府 , 去軍隊 。 」
so i went to the military and asked to borrow 300 radio stations .	所以我去了軍隊 , 要求借3000間無線電站 。
they have more than the government , and they've got more guns than the government .	他們擁有的比政府還要多 , 而且他們擁有的槍比政府還要多 。
so i asked them , could they help us in our fight against hiv .	所以我問他們 , 他們能否協助我們對抗愛滋病 。
and after i gave them statistics , they said , " yes . okay . you can use all the radio stations , television stations . "	在我給他們統計數據之後 , 他們說: 「 沒錯 , 你可以使用所有的電台 , 電視台 。 」
and that's when we went onto the airwaves .	那時我們進入了飛機 。
and then we got a new prime minister soon after that .	接著 , 很快地 , 我們就得到了新首相 。
and he said , " mechai , could you come and join ? "	他說: 「 梅西 , 你能來加入嗎 ? 」
he asked me in because he liked my wife a lot .	他問我 , 因為他很喜歡我太太 。
so i said , " okay . "	所以我說: 「 好吧 。 」
he became the chairman of the national aids committee and increased the budget fiftyfold .	他成了國家愛滋病委員會的主席 , 並增加了五十倍的預算 。
every ministry , even judges , had to be involved in aids education everyone and we said the public , institutions , religious institutions , schools everyone was involved .	每個部長 , 甚至法官 , 都得參與愛滋病教育 , 每一個人 , 我們都說 , 公共、制度、宗教制度 , 每個人都參與 。
and here , every media person had to be trained for hiv .	在這裡 , 每個媒體人員都必須受愛滋病的訓練 。
and we gave every station half a minute extra for advertising to earn more money .	我們給每個站半分鐘的廣告額額外的廣告要賺更多錢 。
so they were happy with that .	所以他們很開心 。
and then aids education in all schools , starting from university .	接著 , 所有學校的愛滋病教育 , 從大學開始 。
and these are high school kids teaching high school kids .	這些是高中生在教高中生 。
and the best teachers were the girls , not the boys , and they were terrific .	最好的老師是那些女孩 , 不是男孩 , 他們很棒 。
and these girls who go around teaching about safe sex and hiv were known as mother theresa .	而這些環繞著教導安全性愛滋病和愛滋病的女孩 , 被稱為 「 母親 」 。
and then we went down one more step .	然後我們再走下一步 。
these are primary school kids third , fourth grade going to every household in the village , every household in the whole of thailand , giving aids information and a condom to every household , given by these young kids .	這些是第一所學校的孩子第三年級 , 四年級 , 在村子裡的每個家庭 , 整個泰國的每個家庭 , 提供艾滋病資訊和保險套給每個家庭 , 給這些孩子 。
and no parents objected , because we were trying to save lives , and this was a lifesaver .	沒有父母反對 , 因為我們試著拯救生命 , 這是個救命 。
and we said , " everyone needs to be involved . "	我們說: 「 每個人都需要參與 。 」
so you have the companies also realizing that sick staff don't work , and dead customers don't buy .	所以 , 公司也意識到 , 生病的員工不行 , 消費者也不買 。
so they all trained .	所以他們都受過訓練 。
and then we have this captain condom , with his harvard mba , going to schools and night spots .	然後我們有了這艘船 , 牠的哈佛大學mba , 上課和夜班 。
and they loved him . you need a symbol of something .	他們喜歡他 , 你需要一個符號
in every country , every program , you need a symbol , and this is probably the best thing he's ever done with his mba .	在每個國家 , 每個國家 , 你都需要一個符號 , 這大概是他對mba做過最好的事 。
and then we gave condoms out everywhere on the streets everywhere , everywhere .	接著 , 我們在街頭各處提供保險套 , 到處都有 。
in taxis , you get condoms .	在計程車中 , 你得到保險套 。
and also , in traffic , the policemen give you condoms our " cops and rubbers " programs .	此外 , 在交通中 , 警察會給你保險套用我們的 「 警察局 」 計畫 。
so , can you imagine new york policemen giving out condoms ?	所以 , 你能想像紐約警察提供保險套嗎 ?
of course i can . and they'd enjoy it immensely ; i see them standing around right now , everywhere .	當然 , 我可以 。 他們會很享受它 , 我看到它們現在站在任何地方 。
imagine if they had condoms , giving out to all sorts of people .	想像一下 , 如果他們有保險套 , 給各式各樣的人 。
and then , new change , we had hair bands , clothing and the condom for your mobile phone during the rainy season .	接著 , 新的改變 , 我們有新的頭髮 , 衣服 , 以及在雨季時 , 手機的保險套 。
and these were the condoms that we introduced .	這些是我們介紹的保險套 。
one says , " weapon of mass protection . "	其中一個說: 「 大規模保護的武器 。 」
we found you know somebody here was searching for the weapon of mass destruction , but we have found the weapon of mass protection: the condom .	我們發現在座有人在尋找大規模毀滅的武器 , 但我們找到了大規模保護的武器:保險套 。
and then it says here , with the american flag , " don't leave home without it . "	上面寫著 , 美國國旗說: 「 不要離開家 。 」
but i have some to give out afterward .	但之後我有一些要放棄 。
but let me warn you , these are thaisized , so be very careful .	但讓我先警告各位 , 這些是泰國化的 , 非常小心 。
and so you can see that condoms can do so many things .	所以你可以看到保險套可以做很多事情 。
look at this i gave this to al gore and to bill senior also .	看看這個 , 我給了高爾和比爾•高爾 。
stop global warming ; use condoms .	停止全球暖化 , 使用保險套 。
and then this is the picture i mentioned to you the weapon of mass protection .	這是我之前提到的大規模保護的武器 。

why just run around ?	為什麼要跑來跑去 ?
and then finally , in thailand we're buddhist , we don't have a god , so instead , we say , " in rubber we trust . "	最後 , 在泰國 , 我們是佛教徒 , 我們沒有上帝 , 所以我們說: 「 橡膠我們相信 。 」
so you can see that we added everything to our endeavor to make life better for the people .	你可以看到 , 我們把一切都加在我們的努力之上 , 讓人民的生活變得更好 。
we had condoms in all the refrigerators in the hotels and the schools , because alcohol impairs judgment .	我們在旅館和學校的冰箱裡都有保險套 , 因為酒精的判斷 。
and then what happened ?	接著發生了什麼事 ?
after all this time , everybody joined in .	在這段時間之後 , 每個人都加入了 。
according to the u . n . , new cases of hiv declined by 90 percent , and according to the world bank , 7 . 7 million lives were saved .	根據聯合國、聯合國、新愛滋病案例減少了90% , 根據世界銀行 , 770萬條生命被拯救 。
otherwise there wouldn't be many thais walking around today .	否則 , 今天沒有多少泰國人走來走去 。
so it just showed you , you could do something about it .	所以它只顯示了你 , 你可以做點什麼 。
90 percent of the funding came from thailand .	90%的資金來自泰國 。
there was political commitment , some financial commitment , and everybody joined in the fight .	有政治承諾 , 有些財務承諾 , 每個人都加入戰鬥 。
so just don't leave it to the specialists and doctors and nurses .	所以 , 不要留給專家、醫生、護士們 。
we all need to help .	我們都需要協助 。
and then we decided to help people out of poverty , now that we got aids somewhat out of the way this time , not with government alone , but in cooperation with the business community .	接著 , 我們決定要幫助人們脫離貧窮 , 現在我們從愛滋病的角度 , 不是政府 , 而是和商業社群合作 。
because poor people are business people who lack business skills and access to credit .	因為窮人是商人 , 他們缺乏商業技能 , 也缺乏信用 。
those are the things to be provided by the business community .	這些都是商業社群提供的 。
we're trying to turn them into barefoot entrepreneurs , little business people .	我們試著把他們變成赤腳企業家 , 商業人士 。
the only way out of poverty is through business enterprise .	脫離貧窮的唯一方法 , 就是透過企業 。
so , that was done .	所以 , 就這樣完成了 。
the money goes from the company into the village via treeplanting .	這筆錢從公司變成了村落的村莊 。
it's not a free gift .	這不是免費的禮物 。
they plant the trees , and the money goes into their microcredit fund , which we call the village development bank .	他們種植樹木 , 資金進入他們的微型信貸基金 , 我們稱之為鄉村發展銀行 。
everybody joins in , and they feel they own the bank , because they have brought the money in .	每個人都加入 , 他們覺得自己擁有銀行 , 因為他們把錢帶進來 。
and before you can borrow the money , you need to be trained .	在你借錢之前 , 你需要受過訓練 。
and we believe if you want to help the poor , those who are living in poverty , access to credit must be a human right .	我們相信 , 如果你想要幫助貧窮的人 , 生活在貧窮中的人 , 能取得信用的人權 , 一定是人權 。
access to credit must be a human right .	信用度必須要是人權 。
otherwise they'll never get out of poverty .	否則他們永遠不會脫離貧困 。
and then before getting a loan , you must be trained .	在貸款之前 , 你必須要受過訓練 。
here's what we call a " barefoot mba , " teaching people how to do business so that , when they borrow money , they'll succeed with the business .	我們稱之為 「 赤腳mba 」 , 教導人們如何做生意 , 這樣 , 當他們借錢時 , 他們就會成功 。
these are some of the businesses: mushrooms , crabs , vegetables , trees , fruits , and this is very interesting nike ice cream and nike biscuits ; this is a village sponsored by nike .	這些是一些企業:蘑菇、螃蟹、蔬菜、樹木、水果 , 這是非常有意思的nike冰淇淋和nike餅乾 ; 這是一個由nike所贊助的村莊 。
they said , " they should stop making shoes and clothes .	他們說: 「 他們應該停止製作鞋子和衣服 。
make these better , because we can afford them . "	把這些做得更好 , 因為我們可以負擔得起 。 」
and then we have silk , thai silk .	然後我們有絲綢 , 泰國絲綢 。
now we're making scottish tartans , as you can see on the left , to sell to all people of scottish ancestors .	現在 , 我們正在做蘇格蘭特蘭泰坦人 , 左邊可以看到 , 賣給所有蘇格蘭祖先 。
so anyone sitting in and watching tv , get in touch with me .	所以 , 任何人坐著看電視 , 跟我聯絡 。
and then this is our answer to starbucks in thailand " coffee and condoms . "	這是我們在泰國的星巴克《咖啡和保險套》的答案 。

your smartphone may feel like a friend but a true friend would give you a smile once in a while . at ted2013 , keller rinaudo demos romo , the smartphonepowered mini robot who can motor along with you on a walk , slide you a cup of coffee across the table , and react to you with programmable expressions .	你的智慧型手機可能感覺像個朋友 , 但一個真正的朋友 , 一陣子會給你微笑一陣子 。 在ted2013年 , 凱爾•里納多•羅莫 , 智慧型飛行機器人 , 可以和你一起散步 , 滑行你一杯咖啡 , 和你一起散步 , 和你產生可編程表情的反應 。

and as it turns out , that's a really hard problem , because you have to build a small , portable robot that's not only really affordable , but it has to be something that people actually want to take home and have around their kids .	結果發現 , 這是個非常困難的問題 , 因為你必須建造一個小型可攜式的機器人 , 不只能負擔得起 , 還需要人們真正想要帶回家 , 帶著孩子們 。
this robot can't be creepy or uncanny .	這種機器人不會很詭異或不可思議 。
he should be friendly and cute .	他應該是友善又可愛的 。
romo's a robot that uses a device you already know and love your iphone as his brain .	romo是一個用你已經知道的裝置和愛你的iphone的機器人 。
and by leveraging the power of the iphone's processor , we can create a robot that is wifi enabled and computer visioncapable for 150 bucks , which is about one percent of what these kinds of robots have cost in the past .	藉由控制iphone處理器的力量 , 我們就能創造出一個可以用wi-fi和電腦視覺的機器人 , 在過去150美元中 , 大約有150美元的機械人所花費的1% 。
when romo wakes up , he's in creature mode .	當romo醒來時 , 他在創作模式中 。

if i duck down , he'll follow me .	如果我搞砸了 , 他會跟著我 。
he's wary , so he'll keep his eyes on me .	他很溫暖 , 所以他會盯著我看 。
if i come over here , he'll turn to follow me .	如果我來這裡 , 他就會跟著我 。
if i come over here he's smart .	如果我來這裡 , 他很聰明 。
and if i get too close to him , he gets scared just like any other creature .	如果我太靠近他 , 他會很害怕和其他生物一樣 。
so in a lot of ways , romo is like a pet that has a mind of his own .	所以 , 在很多方面 , romo就像寵物 , 擁有自己的心靈 。

so he actually streams twoway audio and video between any two smart devices .	所以 , 他實際上是在兩種智慧裝置之間的雙向音頻和影片 。
