let me start by saying , let's look back to the 20th century , and kind of get a sense of how that style of security worked for us .	讓我先說 , 咱們回顧二十世紀 , 了解一下安全對我們來說是如何運作的 。
this is verdun , a battlefield in france just north of the nato headquarters in belgium .	這是佛朗 , 法國的戰場 , 位在比利時的北方 。
at verdun , in 1916 , over a 300day period , 700 , 000 people were killed , so about 2 , 000 a day .	1916年 , 在佛un , 超過300天的時期 , 70萬人死亡 , 每天大約2 , 000人 。
if you roll it forward 20thcentury security into the second world war , you see the battle of stalingrad , 300 days , 2 million people killed .	如果你向前推進20世紀的安全保障 , 進入第二次世界大戰 , 你會看到史達林畢業的戰爭 , 300天 , 有200萬人死亡 。
we go into the cold war , and we continue to try and build walls .	我們進入冷戰 , 我們繼續建造牆壁 。
we go from the trench warfare of the first world war to the maginot line of the second world war , and then we go into the cold war , the iron curtain , the berlin wall .	我們從第一場第一次世界大戰的戰線 , 到第二次世界大戰的黑暗線 , 然後我們進入冷戰 , 鐵幕 , 柏林牆 。
my thesis for us today is , instead of building walls to create security , we need to build bridges .	我今天對我們的論點是 , 與其建設安全的牆壁 , 我們不需要建造橋樑 。
this is a famous bridge in europe .	這是歐洲的一座有名的橋樑 。
it's the bridge over the drina river , the subject of a novel by ivo andrić , and it talks about how , in that very troubled part of europe and the balkans , over time there's been enormous building of walls .	這是dria河的橋樑 , 愛維和里奇的一個小說的主題 , 談到這個令人困擾的歐洲和巴爾幹半島 , 長久以來 , 已經有了巨大的建築牆壁 。
more recently , in the last decade , we begin to see these communities start , hesitatingly , to come together .	更近期 , 在過去十年 , 我們開始看到這些社區開始猶豫地 , 聚在一起 。
i would argue , again , opensource security is about connecting the international , the interagency , the privatepublic , and lashing it together with strategic communication , largely in social networks .	我會說 , 同樣的 , 開放資源的安全性是要把國際、國際、國際間、私人公共組織起來 , 並將它與戰略的溝通結合在一起 , 主要是在社交網路中 。
so let me talk a little bit about why we need to do that , because our global commons is under attack in a variety of ways , and none of the sources of threat to the global commons will be solved by building walls .	所以 , 讓我來談談為什麼我們需要這麼做 , 因為我們的全球公有物在各式各樣的攻擊中 , 沒有任何威脅到全球公有物的來源 , 都不會被建築牆所解決 。
now , i'm a sailor , obviously .	顯然 , 我是航海家 。
this is a ship , a liner , clipping through the indian ocean .	這是一艘船 , 一條線 , 穿過印度洋 。
what's wrong with this picture ?	這張照片有什麼問題 ?
it's got concertina wire along the sides of it .	它沿著它的邊緣有certina電線 。
that's to prevent pirates from attacking it .	這是為了防止海盜攻擊它 。
piracy is a very active threat today around the world . this is in the indian ocean .	像今天是全世界都很活躍的威脅 。 這是在印度洋 。
piracy is also very active in the strait of malacca .	馬拉克卡也非常活躍 。
it's active in the gulf of guinea .	它在幾內亞灣活躍 。
we see it in the caribbean .	我們在加勒比海看到了 。
it's a $10billionayear discontinuity in the global transport system .	它是全球運輸系統的一千億美元不連續性 。
last year , at this time , there were 20 vessels , 500 mariners held hostage .	去年 , 當時有20艘船 , 500名陸軍人持有主人 。
this is an attack on the global commons .	這是全球公有物的攻擊 。
we need to think about how to address it .	我們得要想想要如何處理它 。
let's shift to a different kind of sea , the cyber sea .	讓我們轉換到另一種海洋 , 網路大海 。
here are photographs of two young men .	這是兩位年輕男士的照片 。
at the moment , they're incarcerated .	目前 , 他們被監禁了 。
they conducted a credit card fraud that netted them over 10 billion dollars .	他們做了一個信用卡詐欺 , 把他們關掉超過一百億美金 。
this is part of cybercrime which is a $2trillionayear discontinuity in the global economy .	這是網路犯罪的一部分 , 是全球經濟經濟中2兆美金的損失 。
two trillion a year .	一年兩兆 。
that's just under the gdp of great britain .	這只是英國國內生產毛額下的國內生產毛額 。
so this cyber sea , which we know endlessly is the fundamental piece of radical openness , is very much under threat as well .	所以 , 我們所知的網路海 , 無止盡地是最基本的開放式海域 , 同時也受到威脅 。
another thing i worry about in the global commons is the threat posed by trafficking , by the movement of narcotics , opium , here coming out of afghanistan through europe over to the united states .	關於全球公有物的另一件事 , 我擔心的是人口販賣的威脅 , 是因為毒品、鴉片 , 來自阿富汗 , 從歐洲到美國 。
we worry about cocaine coming from the andean ridge north .	我們擔心從安第斯山脊來的古柯鹼 。
we worry about the movement of illegal weapons and trafficking . above all , perhaps , we worry about human trafficking , and the awful cost of it .	我們擔心非法武器和人口販賣運動 。 最重要的是 , 我們擔心人口販賣 , 以及它的成本 。
trafficking moves largely at sea but in other parts of the global commons .	人口販賣主要在海上 , 但在全球公有物的其他地方 。
this is a photograph , and i wish i could tell you that this is a very hightech piece of us navy gear that we're using to stop the trafficking .	這是一張照片 , 我希望我能告訴你 , 這是一張非常高科技的照片 , 我們用它來阻止人口販賣 。
the bad news is , this is a semisubmersible run by drug cartels .	壞消息是 , 毒品卡特爾的半潛水器是半潛水員 。
it was built in the jungles of south america .	它是在南美的叢林裡建造的 。
we caught it with that lowtech raft — — and it was carrying six tons of cocaine .	我們用那種低科技的軟體捕捉到它 , 帶著六噸的古柯鹼 。
crew of four . sophisticated communications sweep .	船員有四個 , 複雜的通訊 。
this kind of trafficking , in narcotics , in humans , in weapons , god forbid , in weapons of mass destruction , is part of the threat to the global commons .	這種販賣、敘事、人類、武器、上帝禁止大規模毀滅性的武器 , 是對全球公有物的威脅的一部分 。
and let's pull it together in afghanistan today .	咱們今天就在阿富汗總結一下 。
this is a field of poppies in afghanistan .	這是阿富汗的一片餅乾 。
eighty to 90 percent of the world's poppy , opium and heroin , comes out of afghanistan .	世界上80%到90%的貧民窟 , 鴉片和海洛因來自阿富汗 。
we also see there , of course , terrorism .	當然 , 我們也看到了恐怖主義 。
this is where al qaeda is staged from .	這是基地組織的起源 。
we also see a very strong insurgency embedded there .	我們也看到非常強烈的緊急狀況 。
so this terrorism concern is also part of the global commons , and what we must address .	所以 , 這種恐怖主義的擔憂也是全球公有物的一部分 , 我們必須解決的問題 。
so here we are , 21st century .	這裡是21世紀 。
we know our 20thcentury tools are not going to work .	我們知道20世紀的工具行不通 。
what should we do ?	我們該怎麼做 ?
i would argue that we will not deliver security solely from the barrel of a gun .	我認為 , 我們不會只從槍枝的桶子裡提供安全性 。
we will not deliver security solely from the barrel of a gun .	我們不會只從槍枝的桶子裡提供安全性 。
we will need the application of military force .	我們需要軍事力量的應用 。
when we do it , we must do it well , and competently .	當我們這樣做時 , 我們一定要做得很好 , 而且要有能力 。
but my thesis is , opensource security is about international , interagency , privatepublic connection pulled together by this idea of strategic communication on the internet .	但 , 我的論點是 , 開放資源的安全是關於國際的、國際的、私人的連結 , 由網路上策略性溝通的概念所組成的 。
let me give you a couple of examples of how this works in a positive way .	讓我舉幾個例子來說明這個方法是如何運作的 。
this is afghanistan . these are afghan soldiers .	這是阿富汗 , 阿富汗的士兵 。
they are all holding books .	他們都拿著書 。
you should say , " that's odd . i thought i read that this demographic , young men and women in their 20s and 30s , is largely illiterate in afghanistan . "	你應該說: 「 這很奇怪 。 我以為我讀到 , 在20和30年代 , 年輕的男女 , 大部分都在阿富汗 。 」
you would be correct .	你是對的 。
eightyfive percent cannot read when they enter the security forces of afghanistan .	85%的人無法讀取阿富汗的安全力量 。
why ? because the taliban withheld education during the period of time in which these men and women would have learned to read .	為什麼 ? 因為塔利班在這些男人和女人的時期 , 都學會了閱讀 。
so the question is , so , why are they all standing there holding books ?	所以問題是 , 為什麼他們都站在那兒 ?
the answer is , we are teaching them to read in literacy courses by nato in partnership with private sector entities , in partnership with development agencies .	答案是 , 我們在教導他們閱讀文學課程 , 納托和私營企業機構合作 , 與發展機構合作 。
we've taught well over 200 , 000 afghan security forces to read and write at a basic level .	我們已經教了超過二十萬阿富汗的安全性 , 以基本的角度閱讀和寫 。
when you can read and write in afghanistan , you will typically put a pen in your pocket .	當你在阿富汗讀和寫書 , 你通常會把一支筆放在口袋裡 。
at the ceremonies , when these young men and women graduate , they take that pen with great pride , and put it in their pocket .	在儀式中 , 當這些年輕男女和女生畢業時 , 他們很驕傲地把那支筆放進口袋裡 。
this is bringing together international — there are 50 nations involved in this mission — interagency — these development agencies — and privatepublic , to take on this kind of security .	這將國際組織起來 , 有50個國家參與這項任務 , 國際組織--這些發展機構--私人公開 , 採取這種安全 。
now , we are also teaching them combat skills , of course , but i would argue , opensource security means connecting in ways that create longer lasting security effect .	當然 , 我們也在教他們對抗技能 , 但我會說 , 開放式安全意味著連結 , 創造更長久的安全效應 。
this is a us navy warship .	這是美國海軍戰艦 。
it's called the comfort .	它叫做舒適 。
there's a sister ship called the mercy .	有一艘姐妹船叫做 「 慈悲 」 。
they are hospital ships .	他們是醫院的船 。
this one , the comfort , operates throughout the caribbean and the coast of south america conducting patient treatments .	這個 , 舒適的 , 在加勒比海和南美海岸進行病人的治療 。
on a typical cruise , they'll do 400 , 000 patient treatments .	一般來說 , 他們會做四十萬名病人的治療 。
it is crewed not strictly by military but by a combination of humanitarian organizations: operation hope , project smile .	它並沒有嚴格的由軍事組織組成 , 而是人道主義組織的結合:行動希望、計畫微笑 。
other organizations send volunteers .	其他組織發送志願者 。
interagency physicians come out .	診所醫生出來了 。
they're all part of this .	他們都是這方面的一部分 。
to give you one example of the impact this can have , this little boy , eight years old , walked with his mother two days to come to the eye clinic put on by the comfort .	舉個例子 , 這個小男孩 , 八歲的男孩 , 帶著他的母親兩天走到舒適的眼科診所 。
when he was fitted , over his extremely myopic eyes , he suddenly looked up and said , " mama , veo el mundo . "	當他被配戴時 , 他的眼睛非常神秘 , 他突然抬起頭 , 說: 「 媽媽 , 維歐•莫菲歐 。 」
" mom , i see the world . "	「 媽 , 我看到這個世界 。 」
multiply this by 400 , 000 patient treatments , this privatepublic collaboration with security forces , and you begin to see the power of creating security in a very different way .	將它乘上四十萬名病人治療 , 這種私人的合作 , 與安全力量合作 , 你就會開始看到 , 以非常不同的方式創造安全的力量 。
here you see baseball players .	這裡你看到棒球選手 。
can you pick out the two us army soldiers in this photograph ?	你能否從這張照片中挑出兩位美國軍隊士兵 ?
they are the two young men on either side of these young boys . this is part of a series of baseball clinics , where we have explored collaboration between major league baseball , the department of state , who sets up the diplomatic piece of this , military baseball players , who are real soldiers with real skills but participate in this mission , and they put on clinics throughout latin america and the caribbean , in honduras , in nicaragua , in all of the central american and caribbean nations where baseball is so popular , and it creates security .	他們是這些年輕男孩兩邊的兩位年輕人 。 這是一系列棒球診所的一員 , 在那裡 , 我們探索了大聯盟棒球 , 國家的部門 , 設立了外交棒球隊 , 軍事棒球員 , 與真正的技能 , 參與了這個任務 , 他們在拉丁美洲和加勒比美洲 , 加勒比美洲及美洲的所有地方 , 加勒比美洲和美洲的所有地方 , 在加勒比亞的所有地方 , 都在加勒比 , 創造了全國的所有地方 , 以來的巴巴巴巴巴巴巴巴巴拉巴拉斯的美國和美國和美洲和美洲的巴拉巴拉巴拉斯都在各國內部 。
it shows role models to young men and women about fitness and about life that i would argue help create security for us .	它展現了年輕男性和女性的角色 , 關於健身和生活 , 以及我會爭論的人生 , 協助我們創造安全 。
another aspect of this partnership is in disaster relief .	這種合作關係的另一個面向是災難救援 。
this is a us air force helicopter participating after the tsunami in 2004 which killed 250 , 000 people .	這是美國的空軍直升機 , 在2004年海嘯結束後 , 殺死了25萬人 。
in each of these major disasters — the tsunami in 2004 , 250 , 000 dead , the kashmiri earthquake in pakistan , 2005 , 85 , 000 dead , the haitian earthquake , about 300 , 000 dead , more recently the awful earthquaketsunami combination which struck japan and its nuclear industry — in all of these instances , we see partnerships between international actors , interagency , privatepublic working with security forces to respond to this kind of natural disaster .	在這些重大災難中 , 2004年的海嘯 , 25萬人死亡 , 在巴基斯坦 , 2005年 , 8萬5千人死亡 , 海地地地地震 , 近期有30萬人死去 , 最近發生了日本和核子產業的混合 , 在所有這些例子中 , 我們看到了國際演員之間的合作夥伴 , 國際的合作 , 和國際的合作 , 和國際的合作 , 和國際的合作 , 和國際的合作 。

i'll give you another example , and it's how you move this message .	我再舉另一個例子 , 就是你如何傳遞這個訊息 。
i gave a talk like this in london a while back about this point . i said , as i say to all of you , i'm on facebook . friend me .	我在倫敦做過這樣的演講 , 一陣子我跟大家說 , 我在facebook , 朋友我 。
got a little laugh from the audience .	聽眾笑了一點點 。
there was an article which was run by ap , on the wire .	有一篇文章是ap在電線上經營的
got picked up in two places in the world: finland and indonesia .	世界上有兩個地方:芬蘭和印尼 。
the headline was: nato admiral needs friends .	標題是:納托•阿米德需要朋友 。
and the story was a catalyst , and the next morning i had hundreds of facebook friend requests from indonesians and finns , mostly saying , " admiral , we heard you need a friend , and oh , by the way , what is nato ? "	這個故事是催化劑 , 第二天早上 , 我有幾百封臉書的請求 , 來自印尼人和芬恩 , 大多是說: 「 指導者 , 我們聽說你需要朋友 , 喔 , 順道一提 , 娜托是什麼 ? 」
yeah , we laugh , but this is how we move the message , and moving that message is how we connect international , interagency , privatepublic , and these social nets to help create security .	沒錯 , 我們笑了 , 但這就是我們如何傳遞訊息 , 轉動那訊息 , 就是我們如何連結國際、國際性、私密性 , 以及這些社交網路 , 來協助創造安全 。

that is the core of who we are and what we do , and we do it to protect freedom , freedom of speech , all the things we treasure in our societies .	那就是我們是誰的核心 , 我們做的事 , 來保護自由 , 言論自由 , 所有我們在社會中珍惜的東西 。

you don't have to have a military that is either in hard combat or is in the barracks .	你不需要有軍隊在艱難的戰鬥中 , 或在巴拉克 。
i would argue life is a rheostat .	我會爭論人生是一場演說 。
you have to dial it in , and as i think about how we create security in this 21st century , there will be times when we will apply hard power in true war and crisis , but there will be many instances , as we've talked about today , where our militaries can be part of creating 21stcentury security , international , interagency , privatepublic , connected with competent communication .	你必須將之調整起來 , 如同我所想的 , 我們如何在21世紀建立安全性 , 在戰爭和危機中 , 將會有時候 , 將會有好幾次 , 但今天我們已經談到的 , 我們的軍隊可以成為創造21世紀的安全、國際、國際的、私密的、公開的 , 和精密的通訊之間的聯繫 。
i would close by saying that we heard earlier today about wikipedia . i use wikipedia all the time to look up facts , and as all of you appreciate , wikipedia is not created by 12 brilliant people locked in a room writing articles .	最後 , 我會說 , 我們今天聽說過維基百科 , 我常常用維基百科 , 查閱事實 , 就像在座所有人都很感激 , 維基百科都沒有被十二位出色的人鎖在房間寫作文章中 。
wikipedia , every day , is tens of thousands of people inputting information , and every day millions of people withdrawing that information .	維基百科 , 每天都有數以萬計的人在輸入資訊 , 每天有數百萬人在利用這些資訊 。
it's a perfect image for the fundamental point that no one of us is as smart as all of us thinking together .	對根本的意義來說 , 對我們所有人來說 , 這完美的影像 , 沒有一個人會一起思考 。
no one person , no one alliance , no one nation , no one of us is as smart as all of us thinking together .	沒有一個人 , 沒有一個聯盟 , 沒有一個國家 , 沒有一個人像我們所有人一起思考一樣聰明 。
the vision statement of wikipedia is very simple: a world in which every human being can freely share in the sum of all knowledge .	維基的願景非常簡單:一個人都可以自由地分享所有知識的總和 。
my thesis for you is that by combining international , interagency , privatepublic , strategic communication , together , in this 21st century , we can create the sum of all security .	我的論點是 , 把國際、國際、私人、私人、策略性溝通結合在一起 , 在21世紀 , 我們就能創造出所有安全的總結 。
